Life of Imam Ibn Asakir
beginner
5 min
Al-Ash'ari's Writings on Divine Attributes and Vision
Al-Ash'ari lists his works on attributes, vision, and related refutations.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will understand the range and focus of al-Ash'ari's works on divine attributes, the beatific vision, and related doctrinal issues.

Core Idea
Al-Ash'ari authored extensive refutations defending God's attributes and the vision of Him.

In this passage, Ibn 'Asakir transmits al-Ash'ari's own account of his major works concerning the divine attributes and the beatific vision. These works systematically refute the Mu'tazilite and Jahmite positions that deny God's knowledge, power, and other attributes, as well as their rejection of the possibility of seeing God. Al-Ash'ari also engages with anthropomorphist claims and clarifies the correct stance on God's face and hands.

Guided Path
1
Read the Arabic passage
Read the Arabic passage once through to appreciate its enumerative style. Then read the English translation to grasp the range of topics covered.
Notice the repeated phrase 'قال وألفنا' indicating direct speech.
2
Identify the main categories of works
The passage lists several books: on attributes (الصفات), on vision (رؤية الله), on names and rulings (الأسماء والأحكام), and refutations of anthropomorphists (المجسمة). Group these into thematic clusters.
3
Understand the polemical context
Each work targets specific opponents: Mu'tazilah, Jahmiyyah, and those who affirm anthropomorphism. Note how al-Ash'ari defends orthodox positions.
His refutation of the Mu'tazilah on the beatific vision is thorough.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
وألفنا كتابا كبيرا في الاستطاعة على المعتزلة نقضنا فيه استدلالاتهم على أنها قبل الفعل ومسائلهم وجواباتهم، قال وألفنا كتابا كبيرا في الصفات تكلمنا على أصناف المعتزلة والجهمية والمخالفين لنا فيها في نفي علم الله وقدرته وسائر صفاته وعلى أبي الهذيل ومعمر والنظام والفوطى وعلى من قال بقدم العالم وفي فنون كثيرة من فنون الصفات في إثبات الوجه لله واليدين وفي استوائه على العرش وعلى الناشى ومذهبه في الأسماء والصفات، قال وألفنا كتابا في جواز رؤية الله بالأبصار نقضنا فيه جميع اعتلالات المعتزلة في نفيها وإنكارها وإبطالها قال وألفنا كتابا كبيرا ذكرنا فيه اختلاف الناس في الأسماء والأحكام والخاص والعام، قال وألفنا كتابا في الرد على المجسمة وألفنا كتابا آخر في الجسم نرى أن المعتزلة لا يمكنهم أن يجيبوا عن مسائل الجسمية كما يمكننا ذلك وبينا لزوم مسائل الجسمية على أصولهم قال وألفنا كتابا سميناه كتاب إيضاح البرهان في الرد على أهل الزيغ والطغيان جعلناه مدخلا إلى الموجز تكلمنا فيه في الفنون التي تكلمنا فيها في الموجز وألفنا كتابا لطيفا سميناه كتاب اللمع في الرد على أهل الزيغ والبدع وألفنا كتابا سميناه اللمع الكبير جعلناه مدخلا إلى إيضاح البرهان وألفنا اللمع الصغير جعلناه مدخلا إلى اللمع الكبير وألفنا كتابا سميناه كتاب الشرح والتفصيل في الرد على أهل الإفك والتضليل جعلناه للمبتدئين ومقدمة ينظر فيها قبل كتاب اللمع وهو كتاب يصلح للمتعلمين وألفنا كتابا مختصرا جعلناه مدخلا إلى الشرح والتفصيل، قال وألفنا كتابا كبيرا نقضنا فيه الكتاب المعروف بالأصول على محمد بن عبد الوهاب الجبائي كشفنا عن تمويهه في سائر الأبواب التي تكلم فيها من أصول المعتزلة وذكرنا ما للمعتزلة من الحجج في ذلك، بما لم يأت به ونقضنا بحجج الله الزاهرة، وبراهينه الباهرة، يأتي كلامنا عليه في نقضه في جميع مسائل المعتزلة وأجوبتها في الفنون التي اختلفنا نحن وهم فيها، قال وألفنا كتابا كبيرا نقضنا فيه الكتاب المعروف بنقض تأويل الأدلة على البلخي في أصول المعتزلة، وأبنا عن شبهه التي أوردها بأدلة الله الواضحة وأعلامه اللائحة وضممنا إلى ذلك نقض ما ذكره من الكلام في الصفات في عيون المسائل، والجوابات وألفنا كتابا في مقالات المسلمين، يستوعب جميع اختلافهم، ومقالاتهم، وألفنا كتابا في جمل مقالات الملحدين، وجمل أقاويل الموحدين سميناه كتاب جمل المقالات وألفنا كتابا كبيرا في الصفات وهو أكبر كتبه سميناه كتاب الجوابات في الصفات عن مسائل أهل الزيغ والشبهات نقضنا فيه كتابا كنا ألفناه قديما فيها على تصحيح مذهب المعتزلة لم يؤلف لهم كتاب مثله، ثم أبان الله سبحانه لنا الحق فرجعنا عنه فنقضناه وأوضحنا بطلانه، وألفنا كتابا على ابن الراوندي في الصفات، والقرآن وألفنا كتابا نقضنا فيه كتابا للخالدي ألفه في القرآن والصفات قبل أن يؤلف كتابه الملقب بالملخص وألفنا كتابا نقضنا به كتابا للخالدي في إثبات حدث إرادة الله تعالى وأنه شاء ما لم يكن وكان ما لم يشأ وأوضحنا بطلان قوله في ذلك وسميناه القامع لكتاب الخالدي في الإرادة وألفنا كتابا نقضنا فيه كتابا للخالدي في المقالات سماه المهذب سمينا نقضه فيما نخالفه فيه من كتابه الدافع للمهذب ونقضنا كتابا للخالدي نفى فيه رؤية الله تعالى بالأبصار، وألفنا على الخالدي كتابا نقضنا فيه كتابا ألفه في نفي خلق الأعمال وتقديرها عن رب العالمين وألفنا كتابا نقضنا به على البلخي كتابا ذكر أنه أصلح به غلط ابن الراوندي في الجدل، وألفنا كتابا في الاستشهاد أرينا فيه كيف يلزم المعتزلة على محجتهم في الاستشهاد بالشاهد على الغائب أن يثبتوا علم الله وقدرته وسائر صفاته، وألفنا كتابا سميناه المختصر في التوحيد والقدر في أبواب من الكلام منها الكلام في إثبات رؤية الله بالأبصار والكلام في سائر الصفات والكلام في أبواب القدر كلها وفي التولد والتجوير، وسألناهم فيه عن مسائل كثيرة ضاقوا بالجواب عنها ذرعا ولم يجدوا إلى الانفكاك عنها بحجة سبيلا، وألفنا كتابا في شرح أدب الجدل، وألفنا كتابا سميناه كتاب الطبريين في فنون كثيرة من المسائل الكثيرة وألفنا كتابا سميناه جواب الخراسانية في ضروب من المسائل كثيرة، وألفنا كتابا سميناه كتاب الأرجانيين في أبواب مسائل الكلام، وألفنا كتابا سميناه جواب السيرافيين في أجناس من الكلام، وألفنا كتابا سميناه جواب العمانيين في أنواع من الكلام وألفنا كتابا سميناه جواب الجرجانيين في مسائل كانت تدور بيننا وبين
And we authored a great book on capacity (al-istiṭāʿah) against the Muʿtazilah, in which we refuted their arguments that it is before the act, and their questions and answers. He said: And we authored a great book on the attributes (al-ṣifāt), in which we spoke about the categories of the Muʿtazilah, the Jahmiyyah, and those who oppose us in them, regarding their denial of God's knowledge, His power, and the rest of His attributes; and about Abū al-Hudhayl, Muʿammar, al-Naẓẓām, and al-Fuwaṭī; and about those who said the world is eternal; and on many branches of the attributes, in affirming the face of God and the two hands, and His istiwāʾ over the Throne; and about al-Nāshīʾ and his doctrine on names and attributes. He said: And we authored a book on the permissibility of seeing God with the eyes, in which we refuted all the arguments of the Muʿtazilah for denying it, rejecting it, and invalidating it. He said: And we authored a great book in which we mentioned the disagreement of people on names, rulings, the specific and the general. He said: And we authored a book in refutation of the anthropomorphists (al-mujassimah), and another book on the body (al-jism), in which we [argue] that the Muʿtazilah cannot answer the questions of corporeality as we can, and we demonstrated the necessity of the issues of corporeality according to their principles. He said: And we authored a book we named 'The Clarification of the Proof in Refutation of the People of Deviation and Transgression' (Īḍāḥ al-Burhān), which we made an introduction to 'The Compendium' (al-Mūjaz), in which we spoke about the topics we spoke about in 'The Compendium'. And we authored a small book we named 'The Gleams in Refutation of the People of Deviation and Innovation' (al-Lumaʿ), and we authored a book we named 'The Great Gleams' (al-Lumaʿ al-Kabīr), which we made an introduction to 'The Clarification of the Proof', and we authored 'The Small Gleams' (al-Lumaʿ al-Ṣaghīr), which we made an introduction to 'The Great Gleams'. And we authored a book we named 'The Explanation and Detail in Refutation of the People of Falsehood and Misguidance' (al-Sharḥ wa al-Tafṣīl), which we made for beginners and an introduction to be consulted before the book 'al-Lumaʿ', and it is a book suitable for learners. And we authored a concise book which we made an introduction to 'The Explanation and Detail'. He said: And we authored a great book in which we refuted the book known as 'The Principles' (al-Uṣūl) against Muḥammad ibn ʿAbd al-Wahhāb al-Jubbāʾī; we exposed his deception in all the topics in which he spoke on the principles of the Muʿtazilah, and we mentioned what arguments the Muʿtazilah have in that, such that he did not bring, and we refuted with God's flourishing proofs and His overwhelming evidences; our discussion on it in its refutation will come in all the issues of the Muʿtazilah and their answers in the topics in which we and they differed. He said: And we authored a great book in which we refuted the book known as 'Refutation of the Interpretation of Proofs' (Naqḍ Taʾwīl al-Adillah) against al-Balkhī on the principles of the Muʿtazilah, and we explained away the ambiguities he presented with God's clear proofs and manifest signs, and we appended to that a refutation of what he mentioned of speech on attributes in the book 'ʿUyūn al-Masāʾil' and 'al-Jawābāt'. And we authored a book on the sects of the Muslims (maqālāt al-muslimīn), which encompasses all their differences and their doctrines. And we authored a book on the sum of the doctrines of the atheists and the sum of the sayings of the monotheists, which we named 'The Sum of Doctrines' (Jumal al-Maqālāt). And we authored a great book on the attributes—and it is the largest of his books—which we named 'The Responses on Attributes Concerning the Questions of the People of Deviation and Doubts' (al-Jawābāt fī al-Ṣifāt ʿan Masāʾil Ahl al-Zaygh wa al-Shubahāt); in it we refuted a book we had authored earlier on affirming the doctrine of the Muʿtazilah, for which no book like it had been authored for them; then God Almighty made the truth clear to us, so we recanted and refuted it and explained its falsehood. And we authored a book against Ibn al-Rāwandī on attributes and the Qurʾān. And we authored a book in which we refuted a book by al-Khālidī which he authored on the Qurʾān and attributes before he authored his book nicknamed 'al-Mulakhkhaṣ'. And we authored a book with which we refuted a book by al-Khālidī on affirming the temporal origination (ḥudūth) of God's will and that He willed what was not and was what He did not will, and we explained the falsehood of his statement in that, and we named it 'The Repressor of al-Khālidī's Book on Will' (al-Qāmiʿ li-Kitāb al-Khālidī fī al-Irādah). And we authored a book in which we refuted a book by al-Khālidī on doctrines (al-Maqālāt) which he named 'al-Muhadhdhab'; we named its refutation, in what we differed with him in his book, 'al-Dāfiʿ li-l-Muhadhdhab'. And we refuted a book by al-Khālidī in which he denied the vision of God Almighty with the eyes. And we authored against al-Khālidī a book in which we refuted a book he authored on denying the creation of actions and their predestination from the Lord of the worlds. And we authored a book with which we refuted a book by al-Balkhī in which he claimed to have corrected Ibn al-Rāwandī's error in dialectics (al-jadal). And we authored a book on analogy (al-istishhād) in which we showed how the Muʿtazilah are compelled, by their own argument of drawing analogy from the witnessed to the absent, to affirm God's knowledge, power, and the rest of His attributes. And we authored a book we named 'The Compendium on Tawḥīd and Destiny' (al-Mukhtaṣar fī al-Tawḥīd wa al-Qadar) in chapters of kalām, including speech on affirming the vision of God with the eyes, speech on the rest of the attributes, speech on all the chapters of destiny, on generated acts (al-tawallud), and on rendering incapable and equating (al-taʿjīz wa al-tajwīr), and we asked them in it about many questions such that they were straitened for an answer and found no way to escape from them by a proof. And we authored a book on the explanation of the etiquette of dialectics (Sharḥ Adab al-Jadal). And we authored a book we named 'The Book of the Two Ṭabarīs' (Kitāb al-Ṭabarīyayn) on many branches of the many issues. And we authored a book we named 'The Response to the Khurāsāniyyah' (Jawāb al-Khurāsāniyyah) on many kinds of issues. And we authored a book we named 'The Book of the Arjāniyyīn' (Kitāb al-Arjāniyyīn) in chapters of issues of kalām. And we authored a book we named 'The Response to the Sīrāfiyyīn' (Jawāb al-Sīrāfiyyīn) on genera of kalām. And we authored a book we named 'The Response to the ʿUmāniyyīn' (Jawāb al-ʿUmāniyyīn) on types of kalām. And we authored a book we named 'The Response to the Jurjāniyyīn' (Jawāb al-Jurjāniyyīn) on issues that were circulating between us and [them]
Source pages p. 107

Commentary
This passage is a first-person catalog of works authored by Abū al-Ḥasan al-Ashʿarī, as cited by Ibn ʿAsākir in his biographical defense. Al-Ashʿarī recounts his own scholarly output, listing numerous books on kalām topics, each described by its subject and polemical target. The passage begins with a book on istiṭāʿah (capacity) against the Muʿtazilah, wherein he refuted their claim that capacity precedes the act. He then mentions a great book on the divine attributes (ṣifāt), covering refutations of Muʿtazilah, Jahmiyyah, and others who deny God's knowledge, power, and other attributes; specific figures like Abū al-Hudhayl, Muʿammar, al-Naẓẓām, and al-Fuwaṭī are addressed. He also engages with those who posit the eternity of the world and discusses the affirmation of God's face and hands, and His istiwāʾ over the Throne. Next, he lists a book on the beatific vision (ruʾyat Allāh bi-l-abṣār), refuting Muʿtazilī objections. A book on disagreement over names (asmāʾ), rulings (aḥkām), and the specific and general (khāṣṣ wa ʿāmm) follows. He then mentions refutations of anthropomorphists (mujassimah) and a book on the body (jism) arguing that the Muʿtazilah cannot coherently handle corporeality issues. Several works are structured as introductions: 'Īḍāḥ al-Burhān' introduces 'al-Mūjaz'; 'al-Lumaʿ al-Kabīr' introduces 'Īḍāḥ al-Burhān'; 'al-Lumaʿ al-Ṣaghīr' introduces 'al-Lumaʿ al-Kabīr'; and 'al-Sharḥ wa al-Tafṣīl' is for beginners and precedes 'al-Lumaʿ'. A concise work introduces 'al-Sharḥ wa al-Tafṣīl'. He then recounts a large refutation of al-Jubbāʾī's 'al-Uṣūl', exposing deception and presenting counter-arguments. Another refutation targets al-Balkhī's 'Naqḍ Taʾwīl al-Adillah' and includes a critique of his discussion on attributes in 'ʿUyūn al-Masāʾil' and 'al-Jawābāt'. A book on the sects of Muslims (Maqālāt al-Muslimīn) comprehensively covers differences. 'Jumal al-Maqālāt' covers doctrines of atheists and monotheists. Al-Ashʿarī's largest work on attributes, 'al-Jawābāt fī al-Ṣifāt', contains a self-refutation of an earlier work that had supported Muʿtazilī positions, now recanted. He authored against Ibn al-Rāwandī on attributes and the Qurʾān. Several works target al-Khālidī: one on the Qurʾān and attributes (before al-Khālidī's 'al-Mulakhkhaṣ'), one on God's will (al-Irādah), one on doctrines (al-Maqālāt) refuting 'al-Muhadhdhab', one denying the vision of God, one on denying divine creation and predestination of actions. He also refuted al-Balkhī's correction of Ibn al-Rāwandī's error in jadal. A book on al-istishhād demonstrates that the Muʿtazilah's own method of analogy compels them to affirm divine attributes. 'al-Mukhtaṣar fī al-Tawḥīd wa al-Qadar' covers tawḥīd, destiny, vision, attributes, generated acts, and renderings, containing many unanswerable questions for opponents. Finally, he lists works on the etiquette of dialectics, and responses to various groups: 'The Book of the Two Ṭabarīs', 'Jawāb al-Khurāsāniyyah', 'Kitāb al-Arjāniyyīn', 'Jawāb al-Sīrāfiyyīn', 'Jawāb al-ʿUmāniyyīn', and 'Jawāb al-Jurjāniyyīn', which deals with circular issues. The passage ends abruptly mid-sentence.

Misconception & Correction
Misconception: Some think al-Ash'ari only wrote a few works; this passage demonstrates a focused but extensive output on core doctrines.
Correction: Al-Ash'ari authored multiple dedicated works on attributes and vision, showing his systematic defense of orthodoxy.

Checkpoint
Which of the following is NOT a group mentioned in al-Ash'ari's great book on attributes?
A) Mu'tazilah

C) Anthropomorphists

Key Takeaway
Al-Ash'ari authored dedicated works on divine attributes and the beatific vision, systematically refuting opposing views.

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
Al-Ash'ari wrote many works to defend the correct beliefs about God's attributes and the beatific vision. How much time have you dedicated to studying and understanding these foundational beliefs for yourself? Are you content with simply accepting them, or do you strive to know the proofs as Al-Ash'ari did?
?
The passage shows Al-Ash'ari refuting specific Mu'tazilite figures. Have you ever encountered someone who denies that God has attributes or that we will see Him? How did you respond? Were you equipped to defend your faith?
?
Al-Ash'ari not only affirmed God's face, hands, and istiwa' but also wrote against anthropomorphists. Are there times when you imagine God in human-like forms? How can you balance affirming His attributes without falling into anthropomorphism?

Al-Ash'ari's Refutations of al-Jubbai, al-Balkhi, and Others
Al-Ash'ari lists his refutations of specific Mu'tazili scholars.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will understand how al-Ash'ari targeted major Mu'tazili figures with dedicated refutations.

Core Idea
Al-Ash'ari wrote detailed rebuttals of the leading Mu'tazili scholars of his time.

Al-Ash'ari's polemical activity extended beyond generic refutations to specific works aimed at individual scholars. In this passage, he lists books that refute al-Jubbai's 'al-Uṣūl', al-Balkhi's 'Naqḍ Taʾwīl al-Adillah', Ibn al-Rawandi on attributes and the Qur'an, and several works by al-Khalidi on various topics.

Guided Path
1
Identify the opponents
The passage names Muhammad ibn Abd al-Wahhab al-Jubbai, al-Balkhi, Ibn al-Rawandi, and al-Khalidi. Note each one's specific work being refuted.
2
Understand the scope of refutations
Al-Ash'ari refutes al-Jubbai on Mu'tazili principles (al-uṣūl), al-Balkhi on the interpretation of proofs, Ibn al-Rawandi on attributes and the Qur'an, and al-Khalidi on multiple topics including the Qur'an, attributes, will, and creation of actions.
3
Note the self-correction
Al-Ash'ari mentions recanting an earlier work on Mu'tazili theology and writing a refutation of it in his largest book on attributes.
This shows his intellectual development.

وألفنا كتابا كبيرا في الاستطاعة على المعتزلة نقضنا فيه استدلالاتهم على أنها قبل الفعل ومسائلهم وجواباتهم، قال وألفنا كتابا كبيرا في الصفات تكلمنا على أصناف المعتزلة والجهمية والمخالفين لنا فيها في نفي علم الله وقدرته وسائر صفاته وعلى أبي الهذيل ومعمر والنظام والفوطى وعلى من قال بقدم العالم وفي فنون كثيرة من فنون الصفات في إثبات الوجه لله واليدين وفي استوائه على العرش وعلى الناشى ومذهبه في الأسماء والصفات، قال وألفنا كتابا في جواز رؤية الله بالأبصار نقضنا فيه جميع اعتلالات المعتزلة في نفيها وإنكارها وإبطالها قال وألفنا كتابا كبيرا ذكرنا فيه اختلاف الناس في الأسماء والأحكام والخاص والعام، قال وألفنا كتابا في الرد على المجسمة وألفنا كتابا آخر في الجسم نرى أن المعتزلة لا يمكنهم أن يجيبوا عن مسائل الجسمية كما يمكننا ذلك وبينا لزوم مسائل الجسمية على أصولهم قال وألفنا كتابا سميناه كتاب إيضاح البرهان في الرد على أهل الزيغ والطغيان جعلناه مدخلا إلى الموجز تكلمنا فيه في الفنون التي تكلمنا فيها في الموجز وألفنا كتابا لطيفا سميناه كتاب اللمع في الرد على أهل الزيغ والبدع وألفنا كتابا سميناه اللمع الكبير جعلناه مدخلا إلى إيضاح البرهان وألفنا اللمع الصغير جعلناه مدخلا إلى اللمع الكبير وألفنا كتابا سميناه كتاب الشرح والتفصيل في الرد على أهل الإفك والتضليل جعلناه للمبتدئين ومقدمة ينظر فيها قبل كتاب اللمع وهو كتاب يصلح للمتعلمين وألفنا كتابا مختصرا جعلناه مدخلا إلى الشرح والتفصيل، قال وألفنا كتابا كبيرا نقضنا فيه الكتاب المعروف بالأصول على محمد بن عبد الوهاب الجبائي كشفنا عن تمويهه في سائر الأبواب التي تكلم فيها من أصول المعتزلة وذكرنا ما للمعتزلة من الحجج في ذلك، بما لم يأت به ونقضنا بحجج الله الزاهرة، وبراهينه الباهرة، يأتي كلامنا عليه في نقضه في جميع مسائل المعتزلة وأجوبتها في الفنون التي اختلفنا نحن وهم فيها، قال وألفنا كتابا كبيرا نقضنا فيه الكتاب المعروف بنقض تأويل الأدلة على البلخي في أصول المعتزلة، وأبنا عن شبهه التي أوردها بأدلة الله الواضحة وأعلامه اللائحة وضممنا إلى ذلك نقض ما ذكره من الكلام في الصفات في عيون المسائل، والجوابات وألفنا كتابا في مقالات المسلمين، يستوعب جميع اختلافهم، ومقالاتهم، وألفنا كتابا في جمل مقالات الملحدين، وجمل أقاويل الموحدين سميناه كتاب جمل المقالات وألفنا كتابا كبيرا في الصفات وهو أكبر كتبه سميناه كتاب الجوابات في الصفات عن مسائل أهل الزيغ والشبهات نقضنا فيه كتابا كنا ألفناه قديما فيها على تصحيح مذهب المعتزلة لم يؤلف لهم كتاب مثله، ثم أبان الله سبحانه لنا الحق فرجعنا عنه فنقضناه وأوضحنا بطلانه، وألفنا كتابا على ابن الراوندي في الصفات، والقرآن وألفنا كتابا نقضنا فيه كتابا للخالدي ألفه في القرآن والصفات قبل أن يؤلف كتابه الملقب بالملخص وألفنا كتابا نقضنا به كتابا للخالدي في إثبات حدث إرادة الله تعالى وأنه شاء ما لم يكن وكان ما لم يشأ وأوضحنا بطلان قوله في ذلك وسميناه القامع لكتاب الخالدي في الإرادة وألفنا كتابا نقضنا فيه كتابا للخالدي في المقالات سماه المهذب سمينا نقضه فيما نخالفه فيه من كتابه الدافع للمهذب ونقضنا كتابا للخالدي نفى فيه رؤية الله تعالى بالأبصار، وألفنا على الخالدي كتابا نقضنا فيه كتابا ألفه في نفي خلق الأعمال وتقديرها عن رب العالمين وألفنا كتابا نقضنا به على البلخي كتابا ذكر أنه أصلح به غلط ابن الراوندي في الجدل، وألفنا كتابا في الاستشهاد أرينا فيه كيف يلزم المعتزلة على محجتهم في الاستشهاد بالشاهد على الغائب أن يثبتوا علم الله وقدرته وسائر صفاته، وألفنا كتابا سميناه المختصر في التوحيد والقدر في أبواب من الكلام منها الكلام في إثبات رؤية الله بالأبصار والكلام في سائر الصفات والكلام في أبواب القدر كلها وفي التولد والتجوير، وسألناهم فيه عن مسائل كثيرة ضاقوا بالجواب عنها ذرعا ولم يجدوا إلى الانفكاك عنها بحجة سبيلا، وألفنا كتابا في شرح أدب الجدل، وألفنا كتابا سميناه كتاب الطبريين في فنون كثيرة من المسائل الكثيرة وألفنا كتابا سميناه جواب الخراسانية في ضروب من المسائل كثيرة، وألفنا كتابا سميناه كتاب الأرجانيين في أبواب مسائل الكلام، وألفنا كتابا سميناه جواب السيرافيين في أجناس من الكلام، وألفنا كتابا سميناه جواب العمانيين في أنواع من الكلام وألفنا كتابا سميناه جواب الجرجانيين في مسائل كانت تدور بيننا وبين
And we authored a great book on capacity (al-istiṭāʿah) against the Muʿtazilah, in which we refuted their arguments that it is before the act, and their questions and answers. He said: And we authored a great book on the attributes (al-ṣifāt), in which we spoke about the categories of the Muʿtazilah, the Jahmiyyah, and those who oppose us in them, regarding their denial of God's knowledge, His power, and the rest of His attributes; and about Abū al-Hudhayl, Muʿammar, al-Naẓẓām, and al-Fuwaṭī; and about those who said the world is eternal; and on many branches of the attributes, in affirming the face of God and the two hands, and His istiwāʾ over the Throne; and about al-Nāshīʾ and his doctrine on names and attributes. He said: And we authored a book on the permissibility of seeing God with the eyes, in which we refuted all the arguments of the Muʿtazilah for denying it, rejecting it, and invalidating it. He said: And we authored a great book in which we mentioned the disagreement of people on names, rulings, the specific and the general. He said: And we authored a book in refutation of the anthropomorphists (al-mujassimah), and another book on the body (al-jism), in which we [argue] that the Muʿtazilah cannot answer the questions of corporeality as we can, and we demonstrated the necessity of the issues of corporeality according to their principles. He said: And we authored a book we named 'The Clarification of the Proof in Refutation of the People of Deviation and Transgression' (Īḍāḥ al-Burhān), which we made an introduction to 'The Compendium' (al-Mūjaz), in which we spoke about the topics we spoke about in 'The Compendium'. And we authored a small book we named 'The Gleams in Refutation of the People of Deviation and Innovation' (al-Lumaʿ), and we authored a book we named 'The Great Gleams' (al-Lumaʿ al-Kabīr), which we made an introduction to 'The Clarification of the Proof', and we authored 'The Small Gleams' (al-Lumaʿ al-Ṣaghīr), which we made an introduction to 'The Great Gleams'. And we authored a book we named 'The Explanation and Detail in Refutation of the People of Falsehood and Misguidance' (al-Sharḥ wa al-Tafṣīl), which we made for beginners and an introduction to be consulted before the book 'al-Lumaʿ', and it is a book suitable for learners. And we authored a concise book which we made an introduction to 'The Explanation and Detail'. He said: And we authored a great book in which we refuted the book known as 'The Principles' (al-Uṣūl) against Muḥammad ibn ʿAbd al-Wahhāb al-Jubbāʾī; we exposed his deception in all the topics in which he spoke on the principles of the Muʿtazilah, and we mentioned what arguments the Muʿtazilah have in that, such that he did not bring, and we refuted with God's flourishing proofs and His overwhelming evidences; our discussion on it in its refutation will come in all the issues of the Muʿtazilah and their answers in the topics in which we and they differed. He said: And we authored a great book in which we refuted the book known as 'Refutation of the Interpretation of Proofs' (Naqḍ Taʾwīl al-Adillah) against al-Balkhī on the principles of the Muʿtazilah, and we explained away the ambiguities he presented with God's clear proofs and manifest signs, and we appended to that a refutation of what he mentioned of speech on attributes in the book 'ʿUyūn al-Masāʾil' and 'al-Jawābāt'. And we authored a book on the sects of the Muslims (maqālāt al-muslimīn), which encompasses all their differences and their doctrines. And we authored a book on the sum of the doctrines of the atheists and the sum of the sayings of the monotheists, which we named 'The Sum of Doctrines' (Jumal al-Maqālāt). And we authored a great book on the attributes—and it is the largest of his books—which we named 'The Responses on Attributes Concerning the Questions of the People of Deviation and Doubts' (al-Jawābāt fī al-Ṣifāt ʿan Masāʾil Ahl al-Zaygh wa al-Shubahāt); in it we refuted a book we had authored earlier on affirming the doctrine of the Muʿtazilah, for which no book like it had been authored for them; then God Almighty made the truth clear to us, so we recanted and refuted it and explained its falsehood. And we authored a book against Ibn al-Rāwandī on attributes and the Qurʾān. And we authored a book in which we refuted a book by al-Khālidī which he authored on the Qurʾān and attributes before he authored his book nicknamed 'al-Mulakhkhaṣ'. And we authored a book with which we refuted a book by al-Khālidī on affirming the temporal origination (ḥudūth) of God's will and that He willed what was not and was what He did not will, and we explained the falsehood of his statement in that, and we named it 'The Repressor of al-Khālidī's Book on Will' (al-Qāmiʿ li-Kitāb al-Khālidī fī al-Irādah). And we authored a book in which we refuted a book by al-Khālidī on doctrines (al-Maqālāt) which he named 'al-Muhadhdhab'; we named its refutation, in what we differed with him in his book, 'al-Dāfiʿ li-l-Muhadhdhab'. And we refuted a book by al-Khālidī in which he denied the vision of God Almighty with the eyes. And we authored against al-Khālidī a book in which we refuted a book he authored on denying the creation of actions and their predestination from the Lord of the worlds. And we authored a book with which we refuted a book by al-Balkhī in which he claimed to have corrected Ibn al-Rāwandī's error in dialectics (al-jadal). And we authored a book on analogy (al-istishhād) in which we showed how the Muʿtazilah are compelled, by their own argument of drawing analogy from the witnessed to the absent, to affirm God's knowledge, power, and the rest of His attributes. And we authored a book we named 'The Compendium on Tawḥīd and Destiny' (al-Mukhtaṣar fī al-Tawḥīd wa al-Qadar) in chapters of kalām, including speech on affirming the vision of God with the eyes, speech on the rest of the attributes, speech on all the chapters of destiny, on generated acts (al-tawallud), and on rendering incapable and equating (al-taʿjīz wa al-tajwīr), and we asked them in it about many questions such that they were straitened for an answer and found no way to escape from them by a proof. And we authored a book on the explanation of the etiquette of dialectics (Sharḥ Adab al-Jadal). And we authored a book we named 'The Book of the Two Ṭabarīs' (Kitāb al-Ṭabarīyayn) on many branches of the many issues. And we authored a book we named 'The Response to the Khurāsāniyyah' (Jawāb al-Khurāsāniyyah) on many kinds of issues. And we authored a book we named 'The Book of the Arjāniyyīn' (Kitāb al-Arjāniyyīn) in chapters of issues of kalām. And we authored a book we named 'The Response to the Sīrāfiyyīn' (Jawāb al-Sīrāfiyyīn) on genera of kalām. And we authored a book we named 'The Response to the ʿUmāniyyīn' (Jawāb al-ʿUmāniyyīn) on types of kalām. And we authored a book we named 'The Response to the Jurjāniyyīn' (Jawāb al-Jurjāniyyīn) on issues that were circulating between us and [them]
Source pages p. 107

Commentary
This passage is a first-person catalog of works authored by Abū al-Ḥasan al-Ashʿarī, as cited by Ibn ʿAsākir in his biographical defense. Al-Ashʿarī recounts his own scholarly output, listing numerous books on kalām topics, each described by its subject and polemical target. The passage begins with a book on istiṭāʿah (capacity) against the Muʿtazilah, wherein he refuted their claim that capacity precedes the act. He then mentions a great book on the divine attributes (ṣifāt), covering refutations of Muʿtazilah, Jahmiyyah, and others who deny God's knowledge, power, and other attributes; specific figures like Abū al-Hudhayl, Muʿammar, al-Naẓẓām, and al-Fuwaṭī are addressed. He also engages with those who posit the eternity of the world and discusses the affirmation of God's face and hands, and His istiwāʾ over the Throne. Next, he lists a book on the beatific vision (ruʾyat Allāh bi-l-abṣār), refuting Muʿtazilī objections. A book on disagreement over names (asmāʾ), rulings (aḥkām), and the specific and general (khāṣṣ wa ʿāmm) follows. He then mentions refutations of anthropomorphists (mujassimah) and a book on the body (jism) arguing that the Muʿtazilah cannot coherently handle corporeality issues. Several works are structured as introductions: 'Īḍāḥ al-Burhān' introduces 'al-Mūjaz'; 'al-Lumaʿ al-Kabīr' introduces 'Īḍāḥ al-Burhān'; 'al-Lumaʿ al-Ṣaghīr' introduces 'al-Lumaʿ al-Kabīr'; and 'al-Sharḥ wa al-Tafṣīl' is for beginners and precedes 'al-Lumaʿ'. A concise work introduces 'al-Sharḥ wa al-Tafṣīl'. He then recounts a large refutation of al-Jubbāʾī's 'al-Uṣūl', exposing deception and presenting counter-arguments. Another refutation targets al-Balkhī's 'Naqḍ Taʾwīl al-Adillah' and includes a critique of his discussion on attributes in 'ʿUyūn al-Masāʾil' and 'al-Jawābāt'. A book on the sects of Muslims (Maqālāt al-Muslimīn) comprehensively covers differences. 'Jumal al-Maqālāt' covers doctrines of atheists and monotheists. Al-Ashʿarī's largest work on attributes, 'al-Jawābāt fī al-Ṣifāt', contains a self-refutation of an earlier work that had supported Muʿtazilī positions, now recanted. He authored against Ibn al-Rāwandī on attributes and the Qurʾān. Several works target al-Khālidī: one on the Qurʾān and attributes (before al-Khālidī's 'al-Mulakhkhaṣ'), one on God's will (al-Irādah), one on doctrines (al-Maqālāt) refuting 'al-Muhadhdhab', one denying the vision of God, one on denying divine creation and predestination of actions. He also refuted al-Balkhī's correction of Ibn al-Rāwandī's error in jadal. A book on al-istishhād demonstrates that the Muʿtazilah's own method of analogy compels them to affirm divine attributes. 'al-Mukhtaṣar fī al-Tawḥīd wa al-Qadar' covers tawḥīd, destiny, vision, attributes, generated acts, and renderings, containing many unanswerable questions for opponents. Finally, he lists works on the etiquette of dialectics, and responses to various groups: 'The Book of the Two Ṭabarīs', 'Jawāb al-Khurāsāniyyah', 'Kitāb al-Arjāniyyīn', 'Jawāb al-Sīrāfiyyīn', 'Jawāb al-ʿUmāniyyīn', and 'Jawāb al-Jurjāniyyīn', which deals with circular issues. The passage ends abruptly mid-sentence.

Misconception & Correction
Misconception: Al-Ash'ari never revised his own views.
Correction: This passage shows he recanted an earlier work supporting Mu'tazilism and wrote a refutation of it.

Checkpoint
According to this passage, which work by al-Ash'ari includes a recantation of his earlier pro-Mu'tazili book?
A) Refutation of al-Jubbai
B) Al-Jawabat fi al-Sifat
C) Refutation of Ibn al-Rawandi
D) Refutation of al-Khalidi on will

Key Takeaway
Al-Ash'ari wrote targeted refutations against al-Jubbai, al-Balkhi, Ibn al-Rawandi, and al-Khalidi, and also recanted an earlier pro-Mu'tazili work.

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
When was the last time you admitted a major error in your beliefs, especially if it meant rejecting something you once defended passionately? Are you willing to publicly recant a position if God shows you the truth, or does pride prevent you?
?
Al-Ash'ari wrote a book that was the best of its kind for the Mu'tazila, then later refuted it. What cherished idea of yours might need re-examination, and what would it cost you to change?
?
He devoted his life to refuting falsehood after converting. Does your life reflect a similar urgency to defend truth, even against former allies? What step can you take this week to align your actions with that priority?

Life of Imam Ibn Asakir
intermediate
5 min
Al-Ash'ari's Methodological and Regional Polemics
Al-Ash'ari lists his works on methodology, summary works, and regional responses.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will understand al-Ash'ari's works on kalām methodology and his responses to questions from various regions.

Core Idea
Al-Ash'ari also wrote on argumentation, analogy, and addressed theological inquiries from different communities.

In addition to his major refutations, al-Ash'ari composed works on the method of dialectics (jadal) and analogy (istishhad), as well as a comprehensive compendium on tawhid and destiny. He also authored responses to specific groups from Khurasan, Arjan, Siraf, 'Uman, and Jurjan. These show his engagement with broader audiences.

Guided Path
1
Identify the methodological works
Al-Ash'ari wrote on istishhad (analogy) and a compendium on tawhid and destiny. Also a work on the etiquette of jadal.
2
Note the compendium's content
Al-Mukhtasar covers tawhid, destiny, vision, attributes, generated acts, and contains unanswerable questions.
3
Examine the regional responses
He authored books specifically answering questions from Khurasan, Arjan, Siraf, 'Uman, and Jurjan.

علم الله وقدرته وسائر صفاته وعلى أبي الهذيل ومعمر والنظام والفوطى وعلى من قال بقدم العالم وفي فنون كثيرة من فنون الصفات في إثبات الوجه لله واليدين وفي استوائه على العرش وعلى الناشى ومذهبه في الأسماء والصفات، قال وألفنا كتابا في جواز رؤية الله بالأبصار نقضنا فيه جميع اعتلالات المعتزلة في نفيها وإنكارها وإبطالها قال وألفنا كتابا كبيرا ذكرنا فيه اختلاف الناس في الأسماء والأحكام والخاص والعام، قال وألفنا كتابا في الرد على المجسمة وألفنا كتابا آخر في الجسم نرى أن المعتزلة لا يمكنهم أن يجيبوا عن مسائل الجسمية كما يمكننا ذلك وبينا لزوم مسائل الجسمية على أصولهم قال وألفنا كتابا سميناه كتاب إيضاح اللمع الكبير جعلناه مدخلا إلى إيضاح البرهان وألفنا اللمع الصغير جعلناه مدخلا إلى اللمع الكبير وألفنا كتابا سميناه كتاب الشرح والتفصيل في الرد على أهل الإفك والتضليل جعلناه للمبتدئين ومقدمة ينظر فيها قبل كتاب اللمع وهو كتاب يصلح للمتعلمين وألفنا كتابا مختصرا جعلناه مدخلا إلى الشرح والتفصيل، قال وألفنا كتابا كبيرا نقضنا فيه الكتاب المعروف بالأصول على محمد بن عبد الوهاب الجبائي كشفنا عن تمويهه في سائر الأبواب التي تكلم فيها من أصول المعتزلة وذكرنا ما للمعتزلة من الحجج في ذلك، بما لم يأت به ونقضنا بحجج الله الزاهرة، وبراهينه الباهرة، يأتي كلامنا عليه في نقضه في جميع مسائل المعتزلة وأجوبتها في الفنون التي اختلفنا نحن وهم فيها، قال وألفنا كتابا كبيرا نقضنا فيه الكتاب المعروف بنقض تأويل الأدلة على البلخي في أصول المعتزلة، وأبنا عن شبهه التي أوردها بأدلة الله الواضحة وأعلامه اللائحة وضممنا إلى ذلك نقض ما ذكره من الكلام في الصفات في عيون المسائل، والجوابات وألفنا كتابا في مقالات المسلمين، يستوعب جميع اختلافهم، ومقالاتهم، وألفنا كتابا في جمل مقالات الملحدين، وجمل أقاويل الموحدين سميناه كتاب جمل المقالات وألفنا كتابا كبيرا في الصفات وهو أكبر كتبه سميناه كتاب الجوابات في الصفات عن مسائل أهل الزيغ والشبهات نقضنا فيه كتابا كنا ألفناه قديما فيها على تصحيح مذهب المعتزلة لم يؤلف لهم كتاب مثله، ثم أبان الله سبحانه لنا الحق فرجعنا عنه فنقضناه وأوضحنا بطلانه، وألفنا كتابا على ابن الراوندي في الصفات، والقرآن وألفنا كتابا نقضنا فيه كتابا للخالدي ألفه في القرآن والصفات قبل أن يؤلف كتابه الملقب بالملخص وألفنا كتابا نقضنا به كتابا للخالدي في إثبات حدث إرادة الله تعالى وأنه شاء ما لم يكن وكان ما لم يشأ وأوضحنا بطلان قوله في ذلك وسميناه القامع لكتاب الخالدي في الإرادة وألفنا كتابا نقضنا فيه كتابا للخالدي في المقالات سماه المهذب سمينا نقضه فيما نخالفه فيه من كتابه الدافع للمهذب ونقضنا كتابا للخالدي نفى فيه رؤية الله تعالى بالأبصار، وألفنا على الخالدي كتابا نقضنا فيه كتابا ألفه في نفي خلق الأعمال وتقديرها عن رب العالمين وألفنا كتابا نقضنا به على البلخي كتابا ذكر أنه أصلح به غلط ابن الراوندي في الجدل، وألفنا كتابا في الاستشهاد أرينا فيه كيف يلزم المعتزلة على محجتهم في الاستشهاد بالشاهد على الغائب أن يثبتوا علم الله وقدرته وسائر صفاته، وألفنا كتابا سميناه المختصر في التوحيد والقدر في أبواب من الكلام منها الكلام في إثبات رؤية الله بالأبصار والكلام في سائر الصفات والكلام في أبواب القدر كلها وفي التولد والتجوير، وسألناهم فيه عن مسائل كثيرة ضاقوا بالجواب عنها ذرعا ولم يجدوا إلى الانفكاك عنها بحجة سبيلا، وألفنا كتابا في شرح أدب الجدل، وألفنا كتابا سميناه كتاب الطبريين في فنون كثيرة من المسائل الكثيرة وألفنا كتابا سميناه جواب الخراسانية في ضروب من المسائل كثيرة، وألفنا كتابا سميناه كتاب الأرجانيين في أبواب مسائل الكلام، وألفنا كتابا سميناه جواب السيرافيين في أجناس من الكلام، وألفنا كتابا سميناه جواب العمانيين في أنواع من الكلام وألفنا كتابا سميناه جواب الجرجانيين في مسائل كانت تدور بيننا وبين
And we authored a great book on capacity (al-istiṭāʿah) against the Muʿtazilah, in which we refuted their arguments that it is before the act, and their questions and answers. He said: And we authored a great book on the attributes (al-ṣifāt), in which we spoke about the categories of the Muʿtazilah, the Jahmiyyah, and those who oppose us in them, regarding their denial of God's knowledge, His power, and the rest of His attributes; and about Abū al-Hudhayl, Muʿammar, al-Naẓẓām, and al-Fuwaṭī; and about those who said the world is eternal; and on many branches of the attributes, in affirming the face of God and the two hands, and His istiwāʾ over the Throne; and about al-Nāshīʾ and his doctrine on names and attributes. He said: And we authored a book on the permissibility of seeing God with the eyes, in which we refuted all the arguments of the Muʿtazilah for denying it, rejecting it, and invalidating it. He said: And we authored a great book in which we mentioned the disagreement of people on names, rulings, the specific and the general. He said: And we authored a book in refutation of the anthropomorphists (al-mujassimah), and another book on the body (al-jism), in which we [argue] that the Muʿtazilah cannot answer the questions of corporeality as we can, and we demonstrated the necessity of the issues of corporeality according to their principles. He said: And we authored a book we named 'The Clarification of the Proof in Refutation of the People of Deviation and Transgression' (Īḍāḥ al-Burhān), which we made an introduction to 'The Compendium' (al-Mūjaz), in which we spoke about the topics we spoke about in 'The Compendium'. And we authored a small book we named 'The Gleams in Refutation of the People of Deviation and Innovation' (al-Lumaʿ), and we authored a book we named 'The Great Gleams' (al-Lumaʿ al-Kabīr), which we made an introduction to 'The Clarification of the Proof', and we authored 'The Small Gleams' (al-Lumaʿ al-Ṣaghīr), which we made an introduction to 'The Great Gleams'. And we authored a book we named 'The Explanation and Detail in Refutation of the People of Falsehood and Misguidance' (al-Sharḥ wa al-Tafṣīl), which we made for beginners and an introduction to be consulted before the book 'al-Lumaʿ', and it is a book suitable for learners. And we authored a concise book which we made an introduction to 'The Explanation and Detail'. He said: And we authored a great book in which we refuted the book known as 'The Principles' (al-Uṣūl) against Muḥammad ibn ʿAbd al-Wahhāb al-Jubbāʾī; we exposed his deception in all the topics in which he spoke on the principles of the Muʿtazilah, and we mentioned what arguments the Muʿtazilah have in that, such that he did not bring, and we refuted with God's flourishing proofs and His overwhelming evidences; our discussion on it in its refutation will come in all the issues of the Muʿtazilah and their answers in the topics in which we and they differed. He said: And we authored a great book in which we refuted the book known as 'Refutation of the Interpretation of Proofs' (Naqḍ Taʾwīl al-Adillah) against al-Balkhī on the principles of the Muʿtazilah, and we explained away the ambiguities he presented with God's clear proofs and manifest signs, and we appended to that a refutation of what he mentioned of speech on attributes in the book 'ʿUyūn al-Masāʾil' and 'al-Jawābāt'. And we authored a book on the sects of the Muslims (maqālāt al-muslimīn), which encompasses all their differences and their doctrines. And we authored a book on the sum of the doctrines of the atheists and the sum of the sayings of the monotheists, which we named 'The Sum of Doctrines' (Jumal al-Maqālāt). And we authored a great book on the attributes—and it is the largest of his books—which we named 'The Responses on Attributes Concerning the Questions of the People of Deviation and Doubts' (al-Jawābāt fī al-Ṣifāt ʿan Masāʾil Ahl al-Zaygh wa al-Shubahāt); in it we refuted a book we had authored earlier on affirming the doctrine of the Muʿtazilah, for which no book like it had been authored for them; then God Almighty made the truth clear to us, so we recanted and refuted it and explained its falsehood. And we authored a book against Ibn al-Rāwandī on attributes and the Qurʾān. And we authored a book in which we refuted a book by al-Khālidī which he authored on the Qurʾān and attributes before he authored his book nicknamed 'al-Mulakhkhaṣ'. And we authored a book with which we refuted a book by al-Khālidī on affirming the temporal origination (ḥudūth) of God's will and that He willed what was not and was what He did not will, and we explained the falsehood of his statement in that, and we named it 'The Repressor of al-Khālidī's Book on Will' (al-Qāmiʿ li-Kitāb al-Khālidī fī al-Irādah). And we authored a book in which we refuted a book by al-Khālidī on doctrines (al-Maqālāt) which he named 'al-Muhadhdhab'; we named its refutation, in what we differed with him in his book, 'al-Dāfiʿ li-l-Muhadhdhab'. And we refuted a book by al-Khālidī in which he denied the vision of God Almighty with the eyes. And we authored against al-Khālidī a book in which we refuted a book he authored on denying the creation of actions and their predestination from the Lord of the worlds. And we authored a book with which we refuted a book by al-Balkhī in which he claimed to have corrected Ibn al-Rāwandī's error in dialectics (al-jadal). And we authored a book on analogy (al-istishhād) in which we showed how the Muʿtazilah are compelled, by their own argument of drawing analogy from the witnessed to the absent, to affirm God's knowledge, power, and the rest of His attributes. And we authored a book we named 'The Compendium on Tawḥīd and Destiny' (al-Mukhtaṣar fī al-Tawḥīd wa al-Qadar) in chapters of kalām, including speech on affirming the vision of God with the eyes, speech on the rest of the attributes, speech on all the chapters of destiny, on generated acts (al-tawallud), and on rendering incapable and equating (al-taʿjīz wa al-tajwīr), and we asked them in it about many questions such that they were straitened for an answer and found no way to escape from them by a proof. And we authored a book on the explanation of the etiquette of dialectics (Sharḥ Adab al-Jadal). And we authored a book we named 'The Book of the Two Ṭabarīs' (Kitāb al-Ṭabarīyayn) on many branches of the many issues. And we authored a book we named 'The Response to the Khurāsāniyyah' (Jawāb al-Khurāsāniyyah) on many kinds of issues. And we authored a book we named 'The Book of the Arjāniyyīn' (Kitāb al-Arjāniyyīn) in chapters of issues of kalām. And we authored a book we named 'The Response to the Sīrāfiyyīn' (Jawāb al-Sīrāfiyyīn) on genera of kalām. And we authored a book we named 'The Response to the ʿUmāniyyīn' (Jawāb al-ʿUmāniyyīn) on types of kalām. And we authored a book we named 'The Response to the Jurjāniyyīn' (Jawāb al-Jurjāniyyīn) on issues that were circulating between us and [them]
Source pages p. 107

Commentary
This passage is a first-person catalog of works authored by Abū al-Ḥasan al-Ashʿarī, as cited by Ibn ʿAsākir in his biographical defense. Al-Ashʿarī recounts his own scholarly output, listing numerous books on kalām topics, each described by its subject and polemical target. The passage begins with a book on istiṭāʿah (capacity) against the Muʿtazilah, wherein he refuted their claim that capacity precedes the act. He then mentions a great book on the divine attributes (ṣifāt), covering refutations of Muʿtazilah, Jahmiyyah, and others who deny God's knowledge, power, and other attributes; specific figures like Abū al-Hudhayl, Muʿammar, al-Naẓẓām, and al-Fuwaṭī are addressed. He also engages with those who posit the eternity of the world and discusses the affirmation of God's face and hands, and His istiwāʾ over the Throne. Next, he lists a book on the beatific vision (ruʾyat Allāh bi-l-abṣār), refuting Muʿtazilī objections. A book on disagreement over names (asmāʾ), rulings (aḥkām), and the specific and general (khāṣṣ wa ʿāmm) follows. He then mentions refutations of anthropomorphists (mujassimah) and a book on the body (jism) arguing that the Muʿtazilah cannot coherently handle corporeality issues. Several works are structured as introductions: 'Īḍāḥ al-Burhān' introduces 'al-Mūjaz'; 'al-Lumaʿ al-Kabīr' introduces 'Īḍāḥ al-Burhān'; 'al-Lumaʿ al-Ṣaghīr' introduces 'al-Lumaʿ al-Kabīr'; and 'al-Sharḥ wa al-Tafṣīl' is for beginners and precedes 'al-Lumaʿ'. A concise work introduces 'al-Sharḥ wa al-Tafṣīl'. He then recounts a large refutation of al-Jubbāʾī's 'al-Uṣūl', exposing deception and presenting counter-arguments. Another refutation targets al-Balkhī's 'Naqḍ Taʾwīl al-Adillah' and includes a critique of his discussion on attributes in 'ʿUyūn al-Masāʾil' and 'al-Jawābāt'. A book on the sects of Muslims (Maqālāt al-Muslimīn) comprehensively covers differences. 'Jumal al-Maqālāt' covers doctrines of atheists and monotheists. Al-Ashʿarī's largest work on attributes, 'al-Jawābāt fī al-Ṣifāt', contains a self-refutation of an earlier work that had supported Muʿtazilī positions, now recanted. He authored against Ibn al-Rāwandī on attributes and the Qurʾān. Several works target al-Khālidī: one on the Qurʾān and attributes (before al-Khālidī's 'al-Mulakhkhaṣ'), one on God's will (al-Irādah), one on doctrines (al-Maqālāt) refuting 'al-Muhadhdhab', one denying the vision of God, one on denying divine creation and predestination of actions. He also refuted al-Balkhī's correction of Ibn al-Rāwandī's error in jadal. A book on al-istishhād demonstrates that the Muʿtazilah's own method of analogy compels them to affirm divine attributes. 'al-Mukhtaṣar fī al-Tawḥīd wa al-Qadar' covers tawḥīd, destiny, vision, attributes, generated acts, and renderings, containing many unanswerable questions for opponents. Finally, he lists works on the etiquette of dialectics, and responses to various groups: 'The Book of the Two Ṭabarīs', 'Jawāb al-Khurāsāniyyah', 'Kitāb al-Arjāniyyīn', 'Jawāb al-Sīrāfiyyīn', 'Jawāb al-ʿUmāniyyīn', and 'Jawāb al-Jurjāniyyīn', which deals with circular issues. The passage ends abruptly mid-sentence.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Misconception & Correction
Misconception: Al-Ash'ari only wrote against the Mu'tazilah; he also engaged with other groups.
Correction: His works addressed various regional groups with theological questions.

Checkpoint
Which work by al-Ash'ari is described as containing questions that the Mu'tazilah could not answer?
A) Book on istishhad
B) Al-Mukhtasar fi al-Tawhid wa al-Qadar
C) Sharh Adab al-Jadal
D) Jawab al-Khurasaniyyah

Key Takeaway
Al-Ash'ari wrote methodological works on analogy and dialectics, a compendium on tawhid, and responded to theological inquiries from various regions.

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
Do you actively seek answers to your deepest theological questions from scholars who address your specific doubts, or do you settle for generic responses that never truly convict your heart?
?
Al-Ash'ari wrote comprehensive works covering many topics of tawḥīd and destiny. Have you ever undertaken a systematic study of a single Islamic creedal topic until you could defend it with the same clarity?
?
He engaged directly with those who disagreed with him, writing specific responses to their inquiries. Is there a person or community you disagree with whom you have avoided engaging? Will you take a step today to seek understanding, not just victory?

Life of Imam Ibn Asakir
beginner
5 min
Retraction and Refutation: From Mu'tazilism to Orthodoxy
The author describes refuting his own earlier Mu'tazili work in a major book on attributes.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will understand how the author publicly refuted his own earlier Mu'tazili work, demonstrating a commitment to truth and the process of intellectual correction in Islamic theology.

Core Idea
The author's greatest work on attributes was a refutation of his own earlier Mu'tazili writing.

This passage introduces us to a remarkable act of intellectual honesty. The scholar begins by mentioning a comprehensive work summarizing the views of monotheists and atheists, then focuses on a major treatise on the divine attributes. Most strikingly, he reveals that this treatise was written to refute an earlier book of his own that had supported Mu'tazilite doctrine. This lesson explores that pivotal moment of retraction and its significance.

Guided Path
1
Read the passage carefully
Read the Arabic passage once to get the flow. Then read the translation. Notice the two works mentioned: 'Jumal al-Maqalat' and 'al-Jawabat fi al-Sifat'.
2
Identify the retraction narrative
Look for the phrase 'then God showed us the truth, so we retracted it and refuted it and clarified its falseness.' This is the key moment.
This shows the author's willingness to admit error.
3
Reflect on scholarly integrity
Consider why the author would publicly refute his own work. What does this tell us about the value of truth in Islamic scholarship?
It sets a model for intellectual honesty.
4
Connect to the learning objective
How does this passage illustrate the process of intellectual correction?

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
المسلمين، يستوعب جميع اختلافهم ،ومقالاتهم، وألفنا كتابا في جمل مقالات الملحدين، وجمل أقاويل الموحدين سميناه کتاب ( جمل المقالات) وألفنا كتابا كبيرا في الصفات - وهو أكبر كتبه – سمیناه کتاب ( الجوابات فى الصفات عن مسائل أهل الزيغ والشبهات ) نقضنا فيه كتابا كنا ألفناه قديما فيها على تصحيح مذهب المعتزلة لم يؤلف لهم كتاب مثله، ثم أبان الله سبحانه لنا الحق فرجعنا عنه فنقضناه وأوضحنا بطلانه، وألفنا كتابا على ابن الراوندى فى الصفات ،والقرآن وألفنا كتابا نقضنا فيه كتابا للخالدى ألفه في القرآن والصفات قبل ان يؤلف كتابه الملقب . بالملخص وألفنا كتابا نقضنا به كتابا للخالدى فى إثبات حدث إرادة الله تعالى وأنه شاء ما لم يكن وكان مالم يشأ وأوضحنا بطلان قوله في ذلك وسميناه ( القامع لكتاب الخالدى فى الإرادة وألفنا كتابا نقضنا فيه كتابا للخالدى فى المقالات سماه المهذب سمينا نقضه فيما نخالفه فيه من كتابه الدافع للمهذب ) ونقضنا كتابا للخالدى نفى فيه رؤية الله تعالى بالأبصار، وألفنا على الخالدى كتابا نقضنا فيه كتابا ألفه في نفى خلق الأعمال وتقديرها عن رب العالمين وألفنا كتابا نقضنا به على البلخي کتابا ذكر انه أصلح به غلط ابن الراوندى فى الجدل، وألفنا كتابا في الاستشهاد أرينا فيه كيف يلزم المعتزلة على محجتهم فى الاستشهاد بالشاهد على الغائب أن يثبتوا علم الله وقدرته وسائر ،صفاته، وألفنا كتابا سميناه المختصر في التوحيد والقدر فى أبواب من الكلام منها الكلام في إثبات رؤية الله بالأبصار والكلام فى سائر الصفات والكلام في أبواب القدر كلها وفي التولد وفى التعجيز والتجوير، وسألناهم فيه عن مسائل كثيرة ضاقوا بالجواب عنها ذرعا ولم يجدوا إلى الانفكاك عنها بحجة سبيلا، وألفنا كتاباً في شرح أدب الجدل، وألفنا كتابا سميناه ( كتاب الطبريين) وفي فنون كثيرة من المسائل الكثيرة وألفنا كتابا سميناه ( جواب الخراسانية ) في ضروب من المسائل كثيرة ، وألفنا كتابا سميناه ( بكتاب الأرجانيين ) في أبواب مسائل الكلام، وألفنا كتابا سميناه ) جواب السيرافيين) في أجناس من الكلام، وألفنا كتابا سميناه ( جواب العمانيين) في أنواع من الكلام وألفنا كتابا سميناه ) جواب الجرجانيين) في مسائل كانت تدور بيننا وبين المعتزلة، وألفنا كتابا سميناه ( جواب الدمشقيين) في لطائف من الكلام، والفنا كتابا سميناه ) جواب الواسطيين فى فنون من الكلام، وألفنا كتابا سميناه ) جوابات (الرامهرمزيين) وكان بعض المعتزلة من رامهرمز كتب إلى يسألنى الجواب عن مسائل كانت تدور فى نفسه فأجبت عنها، وألفنا كتابا سميناه ( المسائل المنثورة البغدادية ) وفيه مجالس دارت بيننا وبين اعلام المعتزلة، وألفنا كتابا سميناه ( المنتخل ) فى المسائل المنثورات البصريات والفنا كتابا سميته كتاب ( الفنون ) فى الرد على الملحدين، وألفت كتاب النوادر في دقائق الكلام، وألفت كتابا سميته كتاب ( الادراك ) في فنون من لطائف الكلام، وألفت نقض الكتاب المعروف باللطيف على الاسكافي، وألفت كتابا نقضت فيه كلام عباد بن سليمان في دقائق الكلام، وألفت كتابا نقضت فيه كتابا على على بن عيسى من تأليفه، وألفنا كتابا في ضروب من الكلام سميناه ( المختزن) ذكرنا فيه مسائل للمخالفين لم يسألونا عنها ولاسطروها في كتبهم ولم يتجهوا للسؤال وأجبنا عنها بما وفقنا الله تعالى له، وألفنا كتابا فى باب شيء وان الأشياء هى أشياء وان عدمت رجعنا عنه ونقضناه فمن وقع اليه فلا يعولن عليه، وألفنا كتابا في الاجتهاد في الأحكام، وألفنا كتابا فى ان القياس يخص ظاهر القرآن، وألفنا كتابا في المعارف لطيفا، وألفنا كتابا في الأخبار وتخصيصها وألفنا كتابا سميناه ( الفنون ) فى أبواب من الكلام غير كتاب الفنون الذي ألفناه على الملحدين، وألفنا كتابا سميناه ( جواب المصريين ) أتينا فيه على كثير من أبواب الكلام، وألفنا كتابا فى أن العجز عن الشيء غير العجز عن ضده وان ال بجز لا يكون إلا من الموجد نصرنا فيه من قال من أصحابنا بذلك، وألفنا كتابا فيه مسائل على أهل التثنية سميناه كتاب ( المسائل على أهل التثنية ) والفناكتابا مجردا ذكرنا فيه جميع اعتراض الدهريين في قول الموحدين ان الحوادث أولا انها لا تصح وانها لا تصح إلا من محدث وفي أن المحدث واحد وأجبناهم عنه بما فيه اقناع للمسترشدين، وذكرنا أيضا اعتلالات لهم في قدم الأجسام وهذا الكتاب غير كتبنا التي ذكرناها في صدر كتابنا هذا، وه نو مرسوم بالاستقصاء الجميع اعتراض الدهريين وسائر اصناف الملحدين، وألفنا كتابا على الدهريين في اعتلالاتهم فى قدم الأجسام بأنها لا تخلو أن
...of the Muslims, encompassing all their differences and opinions. And we authored a book on the totality of the sayings of the atheists and the totality of sayings of the monotheists, which we named the Book of Total Sayings. And we authored a great book on the attributes—and it is his largest book—which we named the Book of Responses on the Attributes Concerning the Questions of the People of Deviation and Doubts. In it we refuted a book that we had previously authored long ago on correcting the doctrine of the Mu'tazila, for which no book like it had been authored for them. Then God—glorified be He—showed us the truth, so we retracted it and refuted it and clarified its falseness. And we authored a book against Ibn al-Rawandi on the attributes and the Qur'an. And we authored a book in which we refuted a book by al-Khalidi that he authored on the Qur'an and attributes before he authored his book called al-Mulakhkhas. And we authored a book with which we refuted a book by al-Khalidi on proving the temporality of the will of God Most High, and that He willed what was not and was what He did not will, and we clarified the falseness of his statement in that, and we named it al-Qami' li-Kitab al-Khalidi fi al-Irada. And we authored a book in which we refuted a book by al-Khalidi on the theological doctrines (al-maqalat) that he called al-Muhadhdhab. We named its refutation—in what we differ with him in his book—al-Dafi' li-l-Muhadhdhab. And we refuted a book by al-Khalidi in which he denied the vision of God Most High with eyes. And we authored against al-Khalidi a book in which we refuted a book he authored on denying the creation of actions and their predestination from the Lord of the worlds. And we authored a book with which we refuted a book by al-Balkhi that he claimed to have corrected the error of Ibn al-Rawandi in disputation. And we authored a book on istishhad (argument by analogy from the witnessed to the absent) in which we showed how the Mu'tazila are compelled—according to their own proof of arguing from the witnessed to the absent—to affirm the knowledge of God, His power, and the rest of His attributes. And we authored a book we named al-Mukhtasar fi al-Tawhid wa al-Qadar in chapters of kalam, including: speech on proving the vision of God with eyes, speech on the rest of the attributes, speech on all chapters of qadar, on tawallud (generated acts), on ta'jiz (incapacitation) and tajwir (attribution of injustice). And we asked them in it about many questions that they were too constricted to answer and found no way to extricate themselves from them with an argument. And we authored a book on the explanation of the etiquette of disputation. And we authored a book we named the Book of the Tabariyyan, and in it many kinds of numerous issues. And we authored a book we named the Response to the Khurasaniyya in many types of issues. And we authored a book we named the Book of the Arjananiyya in chapters of theological issues. And we authored a book we named the Response to the Sayrafiyya in categories of kalam. And we authored a book we named the Response to the 'Umaniyya in types of kalam. And we authored a book we named the Response to the Jurjaniyya on issues that circulated between us and the Mu'tazila. And we authored a book we named the Response to the Dimashqiyya in subtle points of kalam. And we authored a book we named the Response to the Wasitiyya in genres of kalam. And we authored a book we named the Responses to the Ramhurmuziyya. Some Mu'tazila from Ramhurmuz wrote to me asking for answers to questions that were circulating in his mind, so I answered them. And we authored a book we named the Scattered Baghdadi Issues, and in it are sessions that took place between us and the leading figures of the Mu'tazila. And we authored a book we named al-Muntakhal on the scattered issues of the Basrans. And we authored a book I called the Book of al-Funun in refutation of the atheists. And I authored the Book of al-Nawadir in the subtleties of kalam. And I authored a book I called the Book of al-Idrak in genres of subtle points of kalam. And I authored a refutation of the book known as al-Latif against al-Iskafi. And I authored a book in which I refuted the discourse of 'Abbad ibn Sulayman on the subtleties of kalam. And I authored a book in which I refuted a book by 'Ali ibn 'Isa of his own composition. And we authored a book on categories of kalam called al-Mukhtazan, in which we mentioned issues of the opponents that they neither asked us about nor wrote in their books nor thought to ask, and we answered them according to what God Most High granted us success. And we authored a book on the topic of shay' (thing) and that things are things even if they become non-existent; we retracted it and refuted it, so whoever comes across it should not rely on it. And we authored a book on ijtihad in rulings. And we authored a book on that analogy (qiyas) particularizes the apparent meaning of the Qur'an. And we authored a book on knowledge (ma'arif), a small one. And we authored a book on traditions (akhbar) and their particularization. And we authored a book we named al-Funun in chapters of kalam, different from the Book of al-Funun that we authored against the atheists. And we authored a book we named the Response to the Misriyyin in which we covered many chapters of kalam. And we authored a book on that inability to do a thing is different from inability to do its opposite, and that inability only comes from the existent; in it we supported those of our companions who said that. And we authored a book containing issues against the dualists, which we named the Book of Issues against the Dualists. And we authored a pure book in which we mentioned all the objections of the materialists (dahriyyun) concerning the statement of the monotheists that originated events are not valid first, and that they are not valid except from an originator, and that the originator is one; and we answered them in a way that is convincing for seekers of guidance. And we also mentioned their arguments for the eternity of bodies. And this book is other than our books that we mentioned at the beginning of this our book, and it is marked by comprehensive coverage of all the objections of the materialists and all other types of atheists. And we authored a book against the materialists concerning their arguments for the eternity of bodies—that they must either...
Source pages p. 108

Commentary
This passage is a lengthy and detailed catalogue of theological works authored by the scholar (likely Abu al-Hasan al-Ash'ari, based on the context of Ibn 'Asakir's biography). It serves as a bibliographical record of his polemical and doctrinal writings. The passage begins by stating that the scholar compiled a comprehensive work encompassing all the differing views and articles of the Muslims, and then specifically wrote a book summarizing the statements of atheists and monotheists titled 'Jumal al-Maqalat'. He then lists a major work on the divine attributes, 'al-Jawabat fi al-Sifat', which was a refutation of an earlier work he himself wrote in support of Mu'tazili doctrine, from which he later retracted. This demonstrates his intellectual journey from Mu'tazilism to orthodox Sunni theology. The passage continues enumerating numerous refutations (nuqud) against various individuals such as Ibn al-Rawandi and al-Khalidi, covering topics like the attributes, the Qur'an, the will of God, the vision of God, the creation of actions, and predestination. He also wrote against al-Balkhi and composed a work on istishhad (analogical reasoning from the seen to the unseen) to compel the Mu'tazila to affirm God's attributes. A condensed work on tawhid and qadar is mentioned, containing discussions on the beatific vision, divine attributes, and various aspects of qadar, tawallud, ta'jiz, and tajwir. The author then lists a series of 'responses' (ajwiba) named after different cities or regions (e.g., Khurasaniyya, Arjananiyya, Sayrafiyya, etc.), each addressing specific questions or groups. He also compiled collections of debates (majalis) with Mu'tazili leaders, and wrote works on subtle points of kalam (al-Nawadir, al-Idrak), and refutations of specific opponents like al-Iskafi, 'Abbad ibn Sulayman, and 'Ali ibn 'Isa. The list includes a book on the concept of 'thingness' (shay') that he later retracted, works on ijtihad, qiyas, traditions, and a second 'al-Funun' on kalam. He also authored a comprehensive refutation of the materialists (dahriyyun) and dualists, covering their arguments for the eternity of bodies. The passage emphasizes the breadth and systematic nature of his scholarship, as he addressed virtually every major theological controversy of his time. The commentary should note that this enumeration underscores the author's role as a defender of Sunni orthodoxy through extensive written debate.

Key Terms
المقالات (al-maqalat)
الصفات (al-sifat)
نقض (naqd)
المعتزلة (al-mu'tazila)

Key Terms from Source Passage

Misconception & Correction
Misconception: Scholars never change their positions or retract their earlier writings.
Correction: The author demonstrates that true scholarship involves returning to the truth, even if it means refuting one's own earlier works.

Checkpoint
What did the author do with his earlier book that supported Mu'tazilism?
A) He defended it
B) He expanded it
C) He refuted and retracted it
D) He ignored it

Key Takeaway
The author publicly refuted his own earlier Mu'tazili book to affirm orthodox Islamic theology.

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
Have you ever held a belief that you later realized was wrong, and what did it cost you to retract it? How does the author's public admission of error challenge your own willingness to admit mistakes in matters of faith?
?
The author says 'God showed us the truth, so we retracted it.' When was the last time you truly allowed divine guidance to change a deeply held position, and what steps did you take to correct it?
?
If you had written a book defending a false belief, would you have the courage to write a new book refuting it? What is holding you back from publicly correcting a misunderstanding you once promoted?

Refutations of Individual Opponents: Ibn al-Rawandi, al-Khalidi, and al-Balkhi
The author enumerates refutations against three specific opponents and one constructive work on analogical argument.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will understand the range of refutations the author wrote against specific Mu'tazili and rationalist thinkers.

Core Idea
The author systematically refuted leading opponents like Ibn al-Rawandi and al-Khalidi on key doctrinal issues.

After discussing the retraction of his own earlier work, the author now turns to refutations of other scholars. He lists works written against Ibn al-Rawandi, al-Khalidi, and al-Balkhi, covering topics like the attributes, the Qur'an, the will of God, the vision of God, and the creation of actions. This lesson shows the author's role as a polemicist defending orthodox Ash'ari theology.

Guided Path
1
List the opponents mentioned
Identify the names: Ibn al-Rawandi, al-Khalidi, al-Balkhi. Note that al-Khalidi appears multiple times.
2
Categorize the topics of refutation
For each refutation, note the subject: attributes, Qur'an, will of God, vision, creation of actions, etc.
3
Spot the constructive work
Find the book on istishhad. Unlike the others, this is not a refutation but a positive argument using Mu'tazili methodology.
It shows the author using opponents' methods against them.
4
Reflect on the purpose
Why did the author write multiple refutations of the same person (al-Khalidi)? What does that tell us about the debates of the time?

Commentary

This demonstrates his intellectual journey from Mu'tazilism to orthodox Sunni theology. The passage continues enumerating numerous refutations (nuqud) against various individuals such as Ibn al-Rawandi and al-Khalidi, covering topics like the attributes, the Qur'an, the will of God, the vision of God, the creation of actions, and predestination. He also wrote against al-Balkhi and composed a work on istishhad (analogical reasoning from the seen to the unseen) to compel the Mu'tazila to affirm God's attributes. A condensed work on tawhid and qadar is mentioned, containing discussions on the beatific vision, divine attributes, and various aspects of qadar, tawallud, ta'jiz, and tajwir. The author then lists a series of 'responses' (ajwiba) named after different cities or regions (e.g., Khurasaniyya, Arjananiyya, Sayrafiyya, etc.), each addressing specific questions or groups. He also compiled collections of debates (majalis) with Mu'tazili leaders, and wrote works on subtle points of kalam (al-Nawadir, al-Idrak), and refutations of specific opponents like al-Iskafi, 'Abbad ibn Sulayman, and 'Ali ibn 'Isa. The list includes a book on the concept of 'thingness' (shay') that he later retracted, works on ijtihad, qiyas, traditions, and a second 'al-Funun' on kalam. He also authored a comprehensive refutation of the materialists (dahriyyun) and dualists, covering their arguments for the eternity of bodies. The passage emphasizes the breadth and systematic nature of his scholarship, as he addressed virtually every major theological controversy of his time. The commentary should note that this enumeration underscores the author's role as a defender of Sunni orthodoxy through extensive written debate.

الخالدى (al-Khalidi)
البلخي (al-Balkhi)
الاستشهاد (al-istishhad)
الشاهد والغائب (al-shahid wa al-gha'ib)

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?

The author used the opponent's own method (istishhad) to compel them to accept the truth. Think of a person you know who holds a different belief. Can you identify a point of common ground that might open a door to share the truth with them, rather than simply arguing against their position?

Regional Responses and Comprehensive Works on Kalam
The author lists regional responses, debate collections, and works against materialists and dualists.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will understand the broad geographical and thematic scope of the author's theological works, including responses to various cities and works against materialists and dualists.

Core Idea
The author's writings reached across the Islamic world, responding to specific regional questions and universal atheistic arguments.

The final section of this catalog shows the author's works organized by geography and by topic. He composed books titled after the regions whose scholars had questions: Khurasanis, Arjananis, Sayrafis, 'Umanis, Jurjanis, Damascenes, Wasitis, Ramhurmuzis, and more. He also compiled collections of debates with Mu'tazili leaders, and wrote comprehensive refutations of the materialists (dahriyya) and dualists (tathniyya). This lesson illustrates the global reach of his scholarship.

...of the Muslims, encompassing all their differences and opinions. And we authored a book on the totality of the sayings of the atheists and the totality of sayings of the monotheists, which we named the Book of Total Sayings. And we authored a great book on the attributes—and it is his largest book—which we named the Book of Responses on the Attributes Concerning the Questions of the People of Deviation and Doubts. In it we refuted a book that we had previously authored long ago on correcting the doctrine of the Mu'tazila, for which no book like it had been authored for them. Then God—glorified be He—showed us the truth, so we retracted it and refuted it and clarified its falseness. And we authored a book against Ibn al-Rawandi on the attributes and the Qur'an. And we authored a book in which we refuted a book by al-Khalidi that he authored on the Qur'an and attributes before he authored his book called al-Mulakhkhas. And we authored a book with which we refuted a book by al-Khalidi on proving the temporality of the will of God Most High, and that He willed what was not and was what He did not will, and we clarified the falseness of his statement in that, and we named it al-Qami' li-Kitab al-Khalidi fi al-Irada. And we authored a book in which we refuted a book by al-Khalidi on the theological doctrines (al-maqalat) that he called al-Muhadhdhab. We named its refutation—in what we differ with him in his book—al-Dafi' li-l-Muhadhdhab. And we refuted a book by al-Khalidi in which he denied the vision of God Most High with eyes. And we authored against al-Khalidi a book in which we refuted a book he authored on denying the creation of actions and their predestination from the Lord of the worlds. And we authored a book with which we refuted a book by al-Balkhi that he claimed to have corrected the error of Ibn al-Rawandi in disputation. And we authored a book on istishhad (argument by analogy from the witnessed to the absent) in which we showed how the Mu'tazila are compelled—according to their own proof of arguing from the witnessed to the absent—to affirm the knowledge of God, His power, and the rest of His attributes. And we authored a book we named al-Mukhtasar fi al-Tawhid wa al-Qadar in chapters of kalam, including: speech on proving the vision of God with eyes, speech on the rest of the attributes, speech on all chapters of qadar, on tawallud (generated acts), on ta'jiz (incapacitation) and tajwir (attribution of injustice). And we asked them in it about many questions that they were too constricted to answer and found no way to extricate themselves from them with an argument. And we authored a book on the explanation of the etiquette of disputation. And we authored a book we named the Book of the Tabariyyan, and in it many kinds of numerous issues. And we authored a book we named the Response to the Khurasaniyya in many types of issues. And we authored a book we named the Book of the Arjananiyya in chapters of theological issues. And we authored a book we named the Response to the Sayrafiyya in categories of kalam. And we authored a book we named the Response to the 'Umaniyya in types of kalam. And we authored a book we named the Response to the Jurjaniyya on issues that circulated between us and the Mu'tazila. And we authored a book we named the Response to the Dimashqiyya in subtle points of kalam. And we authored a book we named the Response to the Wasitiyya in genres of kalam. And we authored a book we named the Responses to the Ramhurmuziyya. Some Mu'tazila from Ramhurmuz wrote to me asking for answers to questions that were circulating in his mind, so I answered them. And we authored a book we named the Scattered Baghdadi Issues, and in it are sessions that took place between us and the leading figures of the Mu'tazila. And we authored a book we named al-Muntakhal on the scattered issues of the Basrans. And we authored a book I called the Book of al-Funun in refutation of the atheists. And I authored the Book of al-Nawadir in the subtleties of kalam. And I authored a book I called the Book of al-Idrak in genres of subtle points of kalam. And I authored a refutation of the book known as al-Latif against al-Iskafi. And I authored a book in which I refuted the discourse of 'Abbad ibn Sulayman on the subtleties of kalam. And I authored a book in which I refuted a book by 'Ali ibn 'Isa of his own composition. And we authored a book on categories of kalam called al-Mukhtazan, in which we mentioned issues of the opponents that they neither asked us about nor wrote in their books nor thought to ask, and we answered them according to what God Most High granted us success. And we authored a book on the topic of shay' (thing) and that things are things even if they become non-existent; we retracted it and refuted it, so whoever comes across it should not rely on it. And we authored a book on ijtihad in rulings. And we authored a book on that analogy (qiyas) particularizes the apparent meaning of the Qur'an. And we authored a book on knowledge (ma'arif), a small one. And we authored a book on traditions (akhbar) and their particularization. And we authored a book we named al-Funun in chapters of kalam, different from the Book of al-Funun that we authored against the atheists. And we authored a book we named the Response to the Misriyyin in which we covered many chapters of kalam. And we authored a book on that inability to do a thing is different from inability to do its opposite, and that inability only comes from the existent; in it we supported those of our companions who said that. And we authored a book containing issues against the dualists, which we named the Book of Issues against the Dualists. And we authored a pure book in which we mentioned all the objections of the materialists (dahriyyun) concerning the statement of the monotheists that originated events are not valid first, and that they are not valid except from an originator, and that the originator is one; and we answered them in a way that is convincing for seekers of guidance. And we also mentioned their arguments for the eternity of bodies. And this book is other than our books that we mentioned at the beginning of this our book, and it is marked by comprehensive coverage of all the objections of the materialists and all other types of atheists. And we authored a book against the materialists concerning their arguments for the eternity of bodies—that they must either...

Commentary
This passage is a lengthy and detailed catalogue of theological works authored by the scholar (likely Abu al-Hasan al-Ash'ari, based on the context of Ibn 'Asakir's biography). It serves as a bibliographical record of his polemical and doctrinal writings. The passage begins by stating that the scholar compiled a comprehensive work encompassing all the differing views and articles of the Muslims, and then specifically wrote a book summarizing the statements of atheists and monotheists titled 'Jumal al-Maqalat'. He then lists a major work on the divine attributes, 'al-Jawabat fi al-Sifat', which was a refutation of an earlier work he himself wrote in support of Mu'tazili doctrine, from which he later retracted. This demonstrates his intellectual journey from Mu'tazilism to orthodox Sunni theology. The passage continues enumerating numerous refutations (nuqud) against various individuals such as Ibn al-Rawandi and al-Khalidi, covering topics like the attributes, the Qur'an, the will of God, the vision of God, the creation of actions, and predestination. He also wrote against al-Balkhi and composed a work on istishhad (analogical reasoning from the seen to the unseen) to compel the Mu'tazila to affirm God's attributes. A condensed work on tawhid and qadar is mentioned, containing discussions on the beatific vision, divine attributes, and various aspects of qadar, tawallud, ta'jiz, and tajwir. The author then lists a series of 'responses' (ajwiba) named after different cities or regions (e.g., Khurasaniyya, Arjananiyya, Sayrafiyya, etc.), each addressing specific questions or groups. He also compiled collections of debates (majalis) with Mu'tazili leaders, and wrote works on subtle points of kalam (al-Nawadir, al-Idrak), and refutations of specific opponents like al-Iskafi, 'Abbad ibn Sulayman, and 'Ali ibn 'Isa. The list includes a book on the concept of 'thingness' (shay') that he later retracted, works on ijtihad, qiyas, traditions, and a second 'al-Funun' on kalam. He also authored a comprehensive refutation of the materialists (dahriyyun) and dualists, covering their arguments for the eternity of bodies. The passage emphasizes the breadth and systematic nature of his scholarship, as he addressed virtually every major theological controversy of his time. The commentary should note that this enumeration underscores the author's role as a defender of Sunni orthodoxy through extensive written debate.

المختصر (al-Mukhtasar)
الدهرية (al-dahriyya)
التثنية (al-tathniyya)
الجدل (al-jadal)
التولد (al-tawallud)

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
